\par \b Note: \tab\b0 If you require different COM port settings, you have to change the Docklight
\par \tab project settings. (Menu Tools / Project Settings.. / Tab Communication)
\par \b 
\par Docklight Send Sequences:
\par \b0 On the left side you can find some commands according to the specified ASCII 
\par Protocol. If you want to edit a certain command just double-click on the entry
\par in the Send Sequence list.
\par \b Note: \tab\b0 The light source echoes every single character before processing new
\par \tab characters. This is the reason for 
\par \tab  a) Receive Sequences with <CR> Auto-Reply
\par \tab  b) Intensity commands with Inter-Character-Delay
\par 
\par \b Docklight Receive Sequences:
\par \b0 Docklight can detect certain incoming serial data with the help of definded receive
\par sequences. As an example some Volpi answers will be detected and Docklight
\par reacts on certain echos. \cf1 
\par \cf0 
\par }
